select  i_item_id        ,i_item_desc         ,i_category         ,i_class         ,i_current_price        ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price) as itemrevenue         ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price)*100/sum(sum(cs_ext_sales_price)) over            (partition by i_class) as revenueratio  from	catalog_sales      ,item       ,date_dim  where cs_item_sk = i_item_sk     and i_category in ('Men', 'Home', 'Jewelry')    and cs_sold_date_sk = d_date_sk  and d_date between cast('1999-02-02' as date)   				and (cast('1999-02-02' as date) + interval '30 days')  group by i_item_id          ,i_item_desc           ,i_category          ,i_class          ,i_current_price  order by i_category          ,i_class          ,i_item_id          ,i_item_desc          ,revenueratio limit 100;  
select  i_item_id        ,i_item_desc         ,i_category         ,i_class         ,i_current_price        ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price) as itemrevenue         ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price)*100/sum(sum(cs_ext_sales_price)) over            (partition by i_class) as revenueratio  from	catalog_sales      ,item       ,date_dim  where cs_item_sk = i_item_sk     and i_category in ('Children', 'Shoes', 'Home')    and cs_sold_date_sk = d_date_sk  and d_date between cast('2000-04-16' as date)   				and (cast('2000-04-16' as date) + interval '30 days')  group by i_item_id          ,i_item_desc           ,i_category          ,i_class          ,i_current_price  order by i_category          ,i_class          ,i_item_id          ,i_item_desc          ,revenueratio limit 100;  
select  i_item_id        ,i_item_desc         ,i_category         ,i_class         ,i_current_price        ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price) as itemrevenue         ,sum(cs_ext_sales_price)*100/sum(sum(cs_ext_sales_price)) over            (partition by i_class) as revenueratio  from	catalog_sales      ,item       ,date_dim  where cs_item_sk = i_item_sk     and i_category in ('Books', 'Home', 'Children')    and cs_sold_date_sk = d_date_sk  and d_date between cast('2001-04-28' as date)   				and (cast('2001-04-28' as date) + interval '30 days')  group by i_item_id          ,i_item_desc           ,i_category          ,i_class          ,i_current_price  order by i_category          ,i_class          ,i_item_id          ,i_item_desc          ,revenueratio limit 100;
